<gmapID>0x80857351e5e68d81:0x3066c3bb1a3d72c6< /gmapID><UserId.>109439806230935606681< /UserId.><text>Ok, first off, just telling you how awesome and big this was is impossible so the photo is for scale.

I ordered the Chicken Teriyaki Bowl. That's the small portion... Let me say that again, pictured is the small portion, and it's $5. The large portion items are $7, and I saw one, it's easily twice the size. My girlfriend ordered the Sweet & Sour Chicken, just as big and very yummy. We also got a Ebi Roll, and a Spicy Tuna Roll, all top shelf items with out question.  My only grip is no soda fountain, so we had to get Snapple. But all of that, 2 bowls, 2 rolls, and 2 drinks. $28. I can not tell you how good this food was for the price.

On our way out, we decided heck with it, lets get a smoothie. They are like $3.50 for a small, which is the perfect size. I had a banana and my gf had a mango. It tasted like they just crammed a ton of fruit in there. It was heavy like a milk shake, and tasted like heaven. Soo amazing, and I know I will be showing up again when the weather starts to get warm, like it already is. They do have a large version of the smoothies, and I think thy were like $4.50 or so, and the sign says 64oz, but I saw a few people order them, I think the sign lies, they were HUGE!!! Soo worth it.

In conclusion:
The scary part about this place is how good and cheap it is. It's also right next to the house, just as close as McD's, and basically the same price for a simple meal.< /text>< pictures>

<Review>My mom and I are always on the hunt for exquisite French restaurants. This one is unusual because its upscale and understated at the same time. The dress code is casual and the vide is industrial but country, too, and the food is marvelous.
Just wonderful. I had the Mushroom Tartine and my mom had the Duck Confit Tartine. Both were delicious and just perfectly light and filling. We also each had a basil lemonade which was fantastically refreshing. The parking here is a pain. The lot is tiny and people are going in and out to shop at the surf store next door. Nonetheless I would come back anytime.
The server was attentive.
My mom had taken me here for the croissants which are made fresh daily, but we were too late. Our server indicated they are usually gone by noon. We didn't get seated until 1pm. The wait was only about 20 minutes for a party of 2, and it was definitely worth it (I don't say that often).< /Review>< UserId.>

<username>Scott Kendall< /username><response>None</response><gmap_id>0x80dcf17d9eeebaed:0x1a6963192667f418< /gmap_id>< text>
What a fantastic little spot. We had a great experience dining at Maison.

The staff is extremely friendly and acommodating. They are attentive, know the menu, and are genuine in conversation, even on a busy Sunday. We even took our 21 month old and never felt like a burden.

The menu isn't huge, which is intentional and works well, like your meal is a presentation. It is concise, well thought out, and excellent. Each dish is unique and contributes in it's own way, and the quality of the food is wonderful for such an affordable meal.

Great use of space, pleasing decor and enough elbow room between tables so you aren't sharing your conversation with the rest of the patrons. They frosted the windows, which is a nice touch to diffuse the light throughout the dining room, leaving it cheery and welcoming.

I plan on visiting regularly.<//text>

<Review>This place has a good variety of dishes. There are many options for vegetarian diners and also some gluten-free choices!

I ordered a build your own pasta with penne and a garlic pesto sauce. It was pretty good, but I'll request more sauce next time. It reminded me of Olive Garden a bit. I went late in the evening and have a feeling that earlier would have been better/fresher. The breadstick that came with my meal didn't do anything for me, but maybe I'm just picky. It was a bit dry.

The prices seem a little high, but not unreasonable. I expected a larger portion or higher quality for the 14.95 price. There are refills given on the fountain drinks (which include non-sodas like the delightful pink lemonade I had).

Overall not bad, and it's nice to have an Italian place nearby. I do plan on going again earlier in the day and trying the pizza or calzone.<//Review><gmapID>0x8090c5dea0525901:0x6e19570559c810bd< /gmapID>< Rate>

<review>Swing by here on a hunch to verify some information. After confirming business has exchange hand from G Spot to 3rd Street Tap Room, it's up to introduced myself. This place is still working out the kinks, but from what I've learned, this may eventually turn out as another alternative for after work HH hangout spot. The people running operation are also the same family that runs Internos Wine Bar. As soon as I walked in, the people were friendly and inviting never once rush me to order. There's a couple of televisions and different seating area depending on size of your party. Beer menu automatically changes daily depending on how popular it is. Local and out of state beer are available. What you got today may not be the same tomorrow. Food is served daily from 4-11pm mostly snacks to finger food to main entree of pizza. Great people and good atmosphere with food coming soon makes this the ideal place for me to tucked in and catch up on some work. Btw, WFB ATM is within steps of tap room. You'll never run out of cash for drinks hahaha..<//review><Resp>None< /Resp>< rating>
